<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:освещение.html>освеще́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">osveščénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:освещение.html>освеще́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:освещение.html>освеще́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:освещение.html>освеще́ний</a></b>)

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:освободить.html>освободи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">osvobodítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-тель</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-telʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:освободитель.html>освободи́тель</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">osvobodítelʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:освободитель.html>освободи́теля</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:освободитель.html>освободи́тели</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:освободитель.html>освободи́телей</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">освободи́тельница</b>)
</p>

***освободить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:освободить.html>освободи́ть</a> (2387)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свобода.html>свобо́д</a>(ный)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">svobód(nyj)</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:освободить.html>освободи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">osvobodítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:освобождать.html>освобожда́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to free, to liberate, to emancipate, to set free</li>
<li>to free (from); to exempt (from)</li>
<li>to dismiss</li>
<li>to clear, to empty</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:освободиться.html>освободи́ться</a> (4231)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:освободить.html>освободи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">osvobodítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:освободиться.html>освободи́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">osvobodítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:освобождаться.html>освобожда́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to get free, to break free, to free oneself (from), to get loose</li>
<li>to become empty; to become vacant</li>
<li>to become free, to get free time (e.g. after work)</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:освободить.html>освободи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">osvobodítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:освобождаться.html>освобожда́ться</a> (11247)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:освобождать.html>освобожда́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">osvoboždátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:освобождаться.html>освобожда́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">osvoboždátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:освободиться.html>освободи́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to get free, to break free, to free oneself (from), to get loose</li>
<li>to become empty; to become vacant</li>
<li>to become free, to get free time (e.g. after work)</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:освобождать.html>освобожда́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">osvoboždátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***освобождение.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:освобождение.html>освобожде́ние</a> (3825)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:освобождать.html>освобожда́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">osvoboždátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:освобождение.html>освобожде́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">osvoboždénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:освобождение.html>освобожде́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:освобождение.html>освобожде́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:освобождение.html>освобожде́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>liberation, emancipation, freeing</li>
<li>liberation, deliverance</li>
<li>freeing, vacating (the act of vacating something; moving out of something)</li>
<li>exemption</li></ol>

***освоить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:освоить.html>осво́ить</a> (8192)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>сво́й</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">svój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ить</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-itʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:освоить.html>осво́ить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">osvóitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:осваивать.html>осва́ивать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to master, to cope with <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">making knowledge or method into one's "own"</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to settle, to open up, to develop (new territories)</li>
<li>to develop; to become familiar with the use <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">of lands or machines</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to acclimate <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">in terms of plants</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:освоиться.html>осво́иться</a> (12734)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:освоить.html>осво́ить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">osvóitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:освоиться.html>осво́иться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">osvóitʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:осваиваться.html>осва́иваться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to make oneself familiar <i>(with)</i>, to get the feel <i>(of)</i></li>
<li>to feel comfortable <i>(with)</i>, to adapt <i>(to)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:освоиться.html>осво́иться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:обстановка.html>обстано́вкой</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>osvóitʹsja</b> s obstanóvkoj</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to (begin to) feel at home; adapt to circumstances</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:освоить.html>осво́ить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">osvóitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***освятить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:освятить.html>освяти́ть</a> (23127)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:святой.html>свято́й</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">svjatój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:освятить.html>освяти́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">osvjatítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">освяща́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to sanctify, to hallow, to consecrate
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:освятить.html>освящённый</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:век.html>века́ми</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:время.html>вре́менем</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>osvjaščónnyj</b> vekámi/vrémenem</i> ― <span class="e-translation">time-honoured</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:осевой.html>осево́й</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:вектор.html>ве́ктор</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>osevój</b> véktor</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>axial</b> vector</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***оседать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:оседать.html>оседа́ть</a> (7904)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">осе́д-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">oséd-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оседать.html>оседа́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">osedátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:осесть.html>осе́сть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to settle, to sink</li>
<li>to gravitate</li></ol>

***оседлать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:оседлать.html>оседла́ть</a> (12662)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:седлать.html>седла́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sedlátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оседлать.html>оседла́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">osedlátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:седлать.html>седла́ть</a></b>)
</p>

<li>to straddle</li>
<li>to override</li></ol>

***осенивший.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:осенивший.html>осени́вший</a> (7901)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***осенить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:осенить.html>осени́ть</a> (7901)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From Russian Church Slavonic <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">осенити</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">oseniti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:осенить.html>осени́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">osenítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:осенять.html>осеня́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated<span class="ib-comma">,</span> poetic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to overhang, to spread <i>(above)</i>, to spread as a canopy <i>(over)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:осенить.html>осени́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:себя.html>себя́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:крестный.html>кре́стным</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:знамение.html>зна́мением</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>osenítʹ</b> sebjá kréstnym známenijem</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to cross oneself</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to dawn <i>(upon)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:осенить.html>осени́ло</a></b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:осенить.html>осени́ла</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мысль.html>мысль</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jevó <b>osenílo</b>; jevó <b>oseníla</b> myslʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">it dawned upon him; a thought occurred to him</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***осень.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:осень.html>о́сень</a> (1487)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href = vnd.unilang:осень.html>о́сень</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">osenĭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*(j)esenь</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*h₁es-en-</i>, whence English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">earn</i> and German <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">Ernte</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">harvest</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p><p>Doublet of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">есень</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jesenʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">есеня</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jesenja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belarusian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Belarusian language">Belarusian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="be">во́сень</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="be-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vósjenʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">о́сінь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ósinʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:осень.html>о́сень</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ósenʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:осень.html>о́сени</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:осень.html>о́сени</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:осень.html>о́сеней</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">also figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> autumn, fall</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:осенний.html>осе́нний</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">osénnij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">позднеосе́нний</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">pozdneosénnij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">предосе́нний</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">predosénnij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***осенять.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:осенять.html>осеня́ть</a> (25886)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:осенить.html>осени́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">osenítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-я́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-játʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:осенять.html>осеня́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">osenjátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:осенить.html>осени́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated<span class="ib-comma">,</span> poetic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to overhang, to spread <i>(above)</i>, to spread as a canopy <i>(over)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:осенять.html>осеня́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:себя.html>себя́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:крестный.html>кре́стным</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:знамение.html>зна́мением</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>osenjátʹ</b> sebjá kréstnym známenijem</i> ― <span class="e-translation">cross oneself</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to dawn <i>(upon)</i></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сесть.html>сесть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sestʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
